<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mědь</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">*<a href = vnd.unilang:межа.html>межу́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*mežu</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*meďu</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*médʰyos</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:между.html>ме́жду</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">méždu</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic.

***межа.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:межа.html>межа́</a> (19770)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*meďa</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:межа.html>межа́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mežá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:межа.html>межи́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:межа.html>межи́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:межа.html>ме́жи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:межа.html>меже́й</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:меж.html>меж</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>abutment, abuttal, boundary, margin, division (as in land plots)
<ul><li><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white"><a href = vnd.unilang:лев.html>Лев</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:толстый.html>То́лстой</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:хозяин.html>Хозя́ин</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работник.html>рабо́тник</a></i> 1895:<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:черный.html>чёрное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неподвижный.html>неподви́жно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шевелиться.html>шевели́лось</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:деревня.html>дере́вня</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выросший.html>вы́росший</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:межа.html>меже́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:высокий.html>высо́кий</a> чернобы́льник</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">no čórnoje éto býlo ne nepodvížno, a vsjó ševelílosʹ, i býlo ne derévnja, a výrosšij na <b>mežé</b> vysókij černobýlʹnik</i></dd><dd>that black (thing), however, was not motionless but all too fluttering, and it was not the village but mugwort grown tall at the <b>margin</b></dd></dl></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:междометие.html>междоме́тие</a> (25199)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:между.html>ме́жду</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">méždu</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">between</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метать.html>мета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">metátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to throw</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">interjectiō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:междометие.html>междоме́тие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">meždométije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:междометие.html>междоме́тия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:междометие.html>междоме́тия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:междометие.html>междоме́тий</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:меланхолия.html>меланхо́лия</a> (19065)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:меланхолия.html>меланхо́лия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">melanxólija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:меланхолия.html>меланхо́лии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:меланхолия.html>меланхо́лии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:меланхолия.html>меланхо́лий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>melancholy</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">меланхолик</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">melanxolik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>ме<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:лан.html>лан</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>хо́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 7a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-меланхол-</b>; суффикс: <b>-иj</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-я</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***мелкий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мелкий.html>ме́лкий</a> (881)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">мѣлъкъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mělŭkŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mělъkъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мелкий.html>ме́лкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mélkij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ме́льче</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мельчайший.html>мельча́йший</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>small, tiny, little, minute</li>
<li>small, insignificant, petty, minor</li>
<li>shallow</li>
<li>petty, small-minded</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мелкий.html>ме́лко</a> (6000)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мелкий.html>ме́лкий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mélkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мелкий.html>ме́лко</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mélko</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>shallowly <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in a shallow manner, not deep</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>finely, in small particles, (written) in very small letters (of texts)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мелкий.html>ме́лко</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mélko</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мелкий.html>ме́лкий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mélkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:месть.html>ме́л</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>ко</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> предикатив; неизменяемое.

***мель.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мель.html>мель</a> (14488)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мель.html>мель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">melʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:месть.html>ме́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:месть.html>ме́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мель.html>ме́лей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>shallow, shoal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:месть.html>мели́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na <b>melí</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">in low water, aground; penniless, broke, short of cash <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">literally and figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выброситься.html>вы́броситься</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мель.html>ме́ль</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">výbrositʹsja na <b>mélʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run aground</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снимать.html>снима́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:корабль.html>кора́бль</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:месть.html>ме́ли</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">snimátʹ koráblʹ s <b>méli</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get a ship off, to refloat a ship, to set a ship afloat</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садиться.html>сади́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мель.html>ме́ль</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sadítʹsja na <b>mélʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get into trouble</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посадить.html>посади́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мель.html>ме́ль</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">posadítʹ na <b>mélʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to beach, to strand</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***мелькать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мелькать.html>мелька́ть</a> (3657)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мелькать.html>мелька́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">melʹkátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мелькнуть.html>мелькну́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замелькать.html>замелька́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to flash, to gleam</li>
<li>to flit, to fly past</li>
<li>to loom, to turn up</li>
<li>to appear for a moment, to be glimpsed fleetingly</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замелькать.html>замелька́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zamelʹkátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:примелькаться.html>примелька́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">primelʹkátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промелькнуть.html>промелькну́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">promelʹknútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мель.html>мель</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:мелькнуть.html>мелькну́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-мельк-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***мелькнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мелькнуть.html>мелькну́ть</a> (3165)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From Proto-Indo-European <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mer-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to shimmer, glisten</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">mérkti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to blink, twinkle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μέρα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">méra</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">morning</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌼𐌰𐌿𐍂𐌲𐌹𐌽𐍃</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">maurgins</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">morning</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">morrow</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мелькнуть.html>мелькну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">melʹknútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мелькать.html>мелька́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to flash, to gleam</li>
<li>to flit, to fly (past)</li>
<li>to loom, to turn up</li>
<li>to appear for a moment, to be glimpsed fleetingly</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>мельк<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ну́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 3b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:мелькать.html>мелька́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-мельк-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ну</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
